{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01MYaBxkB23rMxE8hnNBqr8e","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→\"\"\"Pipeline executor -- generic step sequencer with retry, gates, and parallel dispatch.\n     2→\n     3→Composition-via-callable design: consumers (sprint, roadmap) inject their own\n     4→StepRunner and callbacks. The executor handles step ordering, retry logic,\n     5→parallel dispatch, and state management.\n     6→\n     7→NFR-007: No imports from superclaude.cli.sprint or superclaude.cli.roadmap.\n     8→\"\"\"\n     9→\n    10→from __future__ import annotations\n    11→\n    12→import logging\n    13→import threading\n    14→from datetime import datetime, timezone\n    15→from typing import Callable, Protocol\n    16→\n    17→from .gates import gate_passed\n    18→from .models import PipelineConfig, Step, StepResult, StepStatus\n    19→\n    20→_log = logging.getLogger(\"superclaude.pipeline.executor\")\n    21→\n    22→\n    23→class StepRunner(Protocol):\n    24→    \"\"\"Callable that executes a single step's subprocess and returns a result.\n    25→\n    26→    The runner is responsible for:\n    27→    - Launching the claude -p subprocess\n    28→    - Waiting for completion (with timeout enforcement)\n    29→    - Returning a StepResult with appropriate status\n    30→\n    31→    The runner is NOT responsible for:\n    32→    - Retry logic (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    33→    - Gate checking (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    34→    - Step ordering (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    35→    \"\"\"\n    36→\n    37→    def __call__(\n    38→        self,\n    39→        step: Step,\n    40→        config: PipelineConfig,\n    41→        cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n    42→    ) -> StepResult: ...\n    43→\n    44→\n    45→def execute_pipeline(\n    46→    steps: list[Step | list[Step]],\n    47→    config: PipelineConfig,\n    48→    run_step: StepRunner,\n    49→    on_step_start: Callable[[Step], None] = lambda s: None,\n    50→    on_step_complete: Callable[[Step, StepResult], None] = lambda s, r: None,\n    51→    on_state_update: Callable[[dict], None] = lambda state: None,\n    52→    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool] = lambda: False,\n    53→) -> list[StepResult]:\n    54→    \"\"\"Generic pipeline executor.\n    55→\n    56→    Processes steps in order. Each element in ``steps`` is either:\n    57→    - A single Step (executed sequentially)\n    58→    - A list[Step] (all steps in the list executed in parallel)\n    59→\n    60→    For each step:\n    61→    1. Call on_step_start(step)\n    62→    2. Call run_step(step, config, cancel_check)\n    63→    3. If step has gate criteria: run gate_passed()\n    64→    4. If gate fails and attempts < retry_limit: retry (go to 2)\n    65→    5. If gate fails and attempts exhausted: HALT\n    66→    6. Call on_step_complete(step, result)\n    67→    7. Call on_state_update(updated_state_dict)\n    68→\n    69→    For parallel step groups:\n    70→    - All steps in the group run concurrently via _run_parallel_steps()\n    71→    - If any step in the group fails, remaining steps are cancelled\n    72→    - All results from the group must be PASS before proceeding\n    73→\n    74→    Returns list of all StepResults (one per step, flattened).\n    75→    \"\"\"\n    76→    all_results: list[StepResult] = []\n    77→\n    78→    for entry in steps:\n    79→        if cancel_check():\n    80→            break\n    81→\n    82→        if isinstance(entry, list):\n    83→            # Parallel step group\n    84→            for s in entry:\n    85→                on_step_start(s)\n    86→\n    87→            group_results = _run_parallel_steps(entry, config, run_step, cancel_check)\n    88→            all_results.extend(group_results)\n    89→\n    90→            for r in group_results:\n    91→                on_step_complete(r.step, r)\n    92→\n    93→            on_state_update(_build_state(all_results))\n    94→\n    95→            # If any step in the group failed, halt\n    96→            if any(r.status != StepStatus.PASS for r in group_results):\n    97→                break\n    98→        else:\n    99→            # Sequential step\n   100→            result = _execute_single_step(entry, config, run_step, cancel_check, on_step_start, on_step_complete)\n   101→            all_results.append(result)\n   102→            on_state_update(_build_state(all_results))\n   103→\n   104→            if result.status != StepStatus.PASS:\n   105→                break\n   106→\n   107→    return all_results\n   108→\n   109→\n   110→def _execute_single_step(\n   111→    step: Step,\n   112→    config: PipelineConfig,\n   113→    run_step: StepRunner,\n   114→    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n   115→    on_step_start: Callable[[Step], None] = lambda s: None,\n   116→    on_step_complete: Callable[[Step, StepResult], None] = lambda s, r: None,\n   117→) -> StepResult:\n   118→    \"\"\"Execute a single step with retry logic and gate checking.\"\"\"\n   119→    on_step_start(step)\n   120→    max_attempts = step.retry_limit + 1  # If runner already reported failure/timeout, skip gate check\n   152→        if result.status in (StepStatus.TIMEOUT, StepStatus.CANCELLED):\n   153→            on_step_complete(step, result)\n   154→            return result\n   155→\n   156→        # Gate failed\n   171→        _log.info(\"Gate failed for step '%s' (attempt %d/%d): %s\", step.id, attempt, max_attempts, reason)\n   172→\n   173→        if attempt < max_attempts:\n   174→            continue  # retry\n   175→\n   176→        # Exhausted retries\n   177→        result = StepResult(\n   178→            step=step,\n   179→            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n   180→            attempt=attempt,\n   181→            gate_failure_reason=reason,\n   182→            started_at=result.started_at,\n   183→            finished_at=result.finished_at,\n   184→        )\n   185→        on_step_complete(step, result)\n   186→        return result\n   187→\n   188→    # Should not reach here, but safety fallback\n   189→    now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   190→    return StepResult(\n   191→        step=step,\n   192→        status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n   193→        attempt=max_attempts,\n   194→        gate_failure_reason=\"Unexpected: exhausted retry loop\",\n   195→        started_at=now,\n   196→        finished_at=now,\n   197→    )\n   198→\n   199→\n   200→def _run_parallel_steps(\n   201→    steps: list[Step],\n   202→    config: PipelineConfig,\n   203→    run_step: StepRunner,\n   204→    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n   205→) -> list[StepResult]:\n   206→    \"\"\"Run steps concurrently. The executor handles step ordering, retry logic,\nparallel dispatch, and state management.\n\nNFR-007: No imports from superclaude.cli.sprint or superclaude.cli.roadmap.\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport logging\nimport threading\nfrom datetime import datetime, timezone\nfrom typing import Callable, Protocol\n\nfrom .gates import gate_passed\nfrom .models import PipelineConfig, Step, StepResult, StepStatus\n\n_log = logging.getLogger(\"superclaude.pipeline.executor\")\n\n\nclass StepRunner(Protocol):\n    \"\"\"Callable that executes a single step's subprocess and returns a result.\n\n    The runner is responsible for:\n    - Launching the claude -p subprocess\n    - Waiting for completion (with timeout enforcement)\n    - Returning a StepResult with appropriate status\n\n    The runner is NOT responsible for:\n    - Retry logic (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    - Gate checking (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    - Step ordering (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __call__(\n        self,\n        step: Step,\n        config: PipelineConfig,\n        cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n    ) -> StepResult: ...\n\n\ndef execute_pipeline(\n    steps: list[Step | list[Step]],\n    config: PipelineConfig,\n    run_step: StepRunner,\n    on_step_start: Callable[[Step], None] = lambda s: None,\n    on_step_complete: Callable[[Step, StepResult], None] = lambda s, r: None,\n    on_state_update: Callable[[dict], None] = lambda state: None,\n    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool] = lambda: False,\n) -> list[StepResult]:\n    \"\"\"Generic pipeline executor.\n\n    Processes steps in order. Each element in ``steps`` is either:\n    - A single Step (executed sequentially)\n    - A list[Step] (all steps in the list executed in parallel)\n\n    For each step:\n    1. Call on_step_start(step)\n    2. Call run_step(step, config, cancel_check)\n    3. If step has gate criteria: run gate_passed()\n    4. If gate fails and attempts < retry_limit: retry (go to 2)\n    5. If gate fails and attempts exhausted: HALT\n    6. Call on_step_complete(step, result)\n    7. Call on_state_update(updated_state_dict)\n\n    For parallel step groups:\n    - All steps in the group run concurrently via _run_parallel_steps()\n    - If any step in the group fails, remaining steps are cancelled\n    - All results from the group must be PASS before proceeding\n\n    Returns list of all StepResults (one per step, flattened).\n    \"\"\"\n    all_results: list[StepResult] = []\n\n    for entry in steps:\n        if cancel_check():\n            break\n\n        if isinstance(entry, list):\n            # Parallel step group\n            for s in entry:\n                on_step_start(s)\n\n            group_results = _run_parallel_steps(entry, config, run_step, cancel_check)\n            all_results.extend(group_results)\n\n            for r in group_results:\n                on_step_complete(r.step, r)\n\n            on_state_update(_build_state(all_results))\n\n            # If any step in the group failed, halt\n            if any(r.status != StepStatus.PASS for r in group_results):\n                break\n        else:\n            # Sequential step\n            result = _execute_single_step(entry, config, run_step, cancel_check, on_step_start, on_step_complete)\n            all_results.append(result)\n            on_state_update(_build_state(all_results))\n\n            if result.status != StepStatus.PASS:\n                break\n\n    return all_results\n\n\ndef _execute_single_step(\n    step: Step,\n    config: PipelineConfig,\n    run_step: StepRunner,\n    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n    on_step_start: Callable[[Step], None] = lambda s: None,\n    on_step_complete: Callable[[Step, StepResult], None] = lambda s, r: None,\n) -> StepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute a single step with retry logic and gate checking.\"\"\"\n    on_step_start(step)\n    max_attempts = step.retry_limit + 1  # retry_limit=1 means 2 attempts total\n\n    for attempt in range(1, max_attempts + 1):\n        if cancel_check():\n            now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n            result = StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n                attempt=attempt,\n                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n                started_at=now,\n                finished_at=now,\n            )\n            on_step_complete(step, result)\n            return result\n\n        result = run_step(step, config, cancel_check)\n        result = StepResult(\n            step=result.step,\n            status=result.status,\n            attempt=attempt,\n            gate_failure_reason=result.gate_failure_reason,\n            started_at=result.started_at,\n            finished_at=result.finished_at,\n        )\n\n        # If step has no gate, trust the StepRunner's status\n        if step.gate is None:\n            on_step_complete(step, result)\n            return result\n\n        # If runner already reported failure/timeout, skip gate check\n        if result.status in (StepStatus.TIMEOUT, StepStatus.CANCELLED):\n            on_step_complete(step, result)\n            return result\n\n        # Run gate check\n        passed, reason = gate_passed(step.output_file, step.gate)\n        if passed:\n            result = StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=StepStatus.PASS,\n                attempt=attempt,\n                gate_failure_reason=None,\n                started_at=result.started_at,\n                finished_at=result.finished_at,\n            )\n            on_step_complete(step, result)\n            return result\n\n        # Gate failed\n        _log.info(\"Gate failed for step '%s' (attempt %d/%d): %s\", step.id, attempt, max_attempts, reason)\n\n        if attempt < max_attempts:\n            continue  # retry\n\n        # Exhausted retries\n        result = StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n            attempt=attempt,\n            gate_failure_reason=reason,\n            started_at=result.started_at,\n            finished_at=result.finished_at,\n        )\n        on_step_complete(step, result)\n        return result\n\n    # Should not reach here, but safety fallback\n    now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n    return StepResult(\n        step=step,\n        status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n        attempt=max_attempts,\n        gate_failure_reason=\"Unexpected: exhausted retry loop\",\n        started_at=now,\n        finished_at=now,\n    )\n\n\ndef _run_parallel_steps(\n    steps: list[Step],\n    config: PipelineConfig,\n    run_step: StepRunner,\n    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n) -> list[StepResult]:\n    \"\"\"Run steps concurrently. Returns when all complete or one fails.\n\n    Cross-cancellation: if any step fails after retry, a shared Event\n    is set, causing remaining steps to terminate their subprocesses.\n    \"\"\"\n    cancel_event = threading.Event()\n    results: list[StepResult | None] = [None] * len(steps)\n\n    def _worker(idx: int, step: Step) -> None:\n        def combined_cancel() -> bool:\n            return cancel_check() or cancel_event.is_set()\n\n        result = _execute_single_step(step, config, run_step, combined_cancel)\n        results[idx] = result\n        if result.status != StepStatus.PASS:\n            cancel_event.set()\n\n    threads = [\n        threading.Thread(target=_worker, args=(i, s), daemon=True)\n        for i, s in enumerate(steps)\n    ]\n    for t in threads:\n        t.start()\n    for t in threads:\n        t.join()\n\n    # Replace None entries (shouldn't happen, but defensive)\n    final: list[StepResult] = []\n    for i, r in enumerate(results):\n        if r is not None:\n            final.append(r)\n        else:\n            now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n            final.append(StepResult(\n                step=steps[i],\n                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n                attempt=0,\n                gate_failure_reason=\"Thread did not produce a result\",\n                started_at=now,\n                finished_at=now,\n            ))\n\n    return final\n\n\ndef _build_state(results: list[StepResult]) -> dict:\n    \"\"\"Build a state dict from accumulated results.\"\"\"\n    return {\n        \"steps\": {\n            r.step.id: {\n                \"status\": r.status.value,\n                \"attempt\": r.attempt,\n                \"gate_failure_reason\": r.gate_failure_reason,\n            }\n            for r in results\n        },\n        \"total\": len(results),\n        \"passed\": sum(1 for r in results if r.status == StepStatus.PASS),\n        \"failed\": sum(1 for r in results if r.status.is_failure),\n    }\n","numLines":266,"startLine":1,"totalLines":266}}}
